class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1376663' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1376663?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论宦官不必尽诛</a><span class='authorDate'>（901年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐末 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21436, "唐末", "韩偓", "poem_title_1376663")'>韩偓</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1376663_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1376663'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1376663'>东内之变。敕使谁非同恶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1376663_comment'></div>处之当在正旦。今已失其时矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1376663_comment'></div>臣见陛下诏书云。自刘季述等四家之外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1376663_comment'></div>其馀一无所问。夫人主所重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1376663_comment'></div>莫大于信。既下此诏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1376663_comment'></div>则守之宜坚。若复戮一人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1376663_comment'></div>则人人惧死矣。然后来所去者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1376663_comment'></div>已为不少。此其所以恟恟不安也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1376663_comment'></div>陛下不若择其尤无良者数人。明示其罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1376663_comment'></div>置之于法。然后抚论其馀曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1376663_comment'></div>吾恐尔曹谓吾心有所贮。自今无可疑矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1376663_comment'></div>乃择其忠厚者。使为之长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1376663_comment'></div>其徒有善则奖之。有罪则惩之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1376663_comment'></div>咸自安矣。今此曹在公私者以万数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1376663_comment'></div>岂可尽诛邪。夫帝王之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1376663_comment'></div>当以重厚镇之。公正御之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1376663_comment'></div>至于琐细机巧。此机生则彼机应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1376663_comment'></div>以终不能成大功。所谓理丝而棼之者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1376663_comment'></div>况今朝廷之权。散在四方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1376663_comment'></div>苟能先收此权。则事无不可为者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1376663_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1376663_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=901&endYear=901')">901年</a>　韩偓在朝中，有文多篇。作品：《韩偓对话录》第三则。《韩偓对话录》第四则。<br /><a href="javascript: id='poem_sentence_2_49001_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=901&endYear=901')">901年</a>　韩偓与诗友们互相唱和，有《无题四首》（包括《倒押前韵》）<div id='poem_49259' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_49259' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/49259?labeling=true' target='_blank'>无题<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（901年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐末 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21436, "唐末", "韩偓", "poem_title_49259")'>韩偓</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_49259_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_49259'>余辛酉年戏作无题十四韵，故奉常王公向国首于继和，故内翰吴侍郎融、令狐舍人涣、阁下刘舍人崇誉、吏部王员外涣相次属和。余因作第二首，却寄诸公，二内翰及小天亦再和。余复作第三首，二内翰亦三和，王公一首，刘紫微一首，王小天一首，二学士各三首。余又倒押前韵成第四首，二学士笑谓余曰：「谨竖降旗，何朱研如是也？」遂绝笔。是岁十月末，余在内直，一旦兵起，随驾西狩，文稿咸弃，更无孓遗。丙寅年九月，在福建寓止，有前东都度支院苏炜端公，挈余沦落诗稿见授，中得无题一首。因追味旧作，缺忘甚多，唯第二第四首彷佛可记，其第三首才得数句而已。今亦依次编之，以俟他时偶获全本，馀五人所和，不复忆省矣。</div><div id='poem_preface_49259_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_allusion_49259'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(1788, "poem_allusion_49259")'>东邻</span>　<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(4254, "poem_allusion_49259")'>金屋</span></div><div id='poem_allusion_49259_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_49259'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_49259'>小槛移<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_49259", 49259, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>灯灺</span>，空房锁隙尘。<div id='poem_sentence_0_49259_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_49259'>额波<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作披）</span>风尽日，帘影<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作匝，又作押）</span>月侵晨。<div id='poem_sentence_1_49259_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_49259'>香辣<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作瓣）</span>更衣后，钗梁拢鬓新。<div id='poem_sentence_2_49259_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_49259'>吉音闻诡计，醉语近天真。<div id='poem_sentence_6_49259_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_49259'>歌凝眉际恨，酒发脸边春。<div id='poem_sentence_7_49259_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_49259'>溪纻殊倾<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作轻）</span>越，楼箫岂<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作却）</span>羡秦。<div id='poem_sentence_8_49259_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_49259_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_49259'>乐府降清唱，宫厨减食珍。<div id='poem_sentence_10_49259_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' 江夏

id='poem_sentence_0_49231_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_49231'>忍苦可能遭鬼笑，息机应免致鸥猜。<div id='poem_sentence_1_49231_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_49231'>岳僧互乞新诗去，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_49231", 49231, "Clauses/5/Comments/0")'>酒保</span>频徵旧债来。<div id='poem_sentence_2_49231_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_49231'>唯有狂吟与沈饮，时时犹自触灵台。<div id='poem_sentence_3_49231_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_49174_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_49174'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_49174'>天似空江星似波，时时珠露滴圆荷。<div id='poem_sentence_0_49174_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_49174'>平生踪迹慕真隐，此夕襟怀深自多。<div id='poem_sentence_1_49174_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_49174'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_49174", 49174, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>格是</span>厌厌饶酒病，终须<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_49174", 49174, "Clauses/5/Comments/0")'>的的</span>学渔歌。<div id='poem_sentence_2_49174_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_49174'>无名无位堪休去，犹拟朝衣换钓蓑。<div id='poem_sentence_3_49174_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_49174'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_49174_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>

-----title
抚州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='39d7ba2c236549f8b0f136745fe83b88_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("39d7ba2c236549f8b0f136745fe83b88");'><span id='39d7ba2c236549f8b0f136745fe83b88_link' id='poem_sentence_4_49121_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=906&endYear=906')">906年2月</a>　韩偓本年二月已至江西抚州，有赠危全讽司空诗。作品：《和王舍人抚州饮席赠韦司空》<span 南城

建瓯

<div class='label1' id='099990675ff14958a4597c5e43e19845_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("099990675ff14958a4597c5e43e19845");'><span id='099990675ff14958a4597c5e43e19845_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=909&endYear=909')">909年</a>，68岁</div><div id='099990675ff14958a4597c5e43e19845' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>在福州。韩偓作梦后，有诗。作品：《梦中作》<div id='poem_49228' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_49228' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/49228?labeling=true' target='_blank'>梦中作</a><span class='authorDate'>（909年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐末 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21436, "唐末", "韩偓", "poem_title_49228")'>韩偓</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_49228_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_49228'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_49228'>紫宸初启列<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_49228", 49228, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>鸳鸾</span>，直向龙墀对揖班。<div id='poem_sentence_0_49228_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_49228'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_49228", 49228, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>九曜</span>再新环北极，万方依旧祝南山。<div id='poem_sentence_1_49228_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_49228'>礼容<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_49228", 49228, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>肃睦</span>缨緌外，和气熏蒸剑履间。<div id='poem_sentence_2_49228_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_49228'>扇合却循黄道退，庙堂谈笑百司闲。<div id='poem_sentence_3_49228_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_49228'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_49228_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>

-----title
尤溪
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='8d05478618b14570a2f3a4f5177b14ee_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("8d05478618b14570a2f3a4f5177b14ee");'><span id='8d05478618b14570a2f3a4f5177b14ee_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=910&endYear=910')">910年</a>，69岁</div><div id='8d05478618b14570a2f3a4f5177b14ee' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>韩偓抵达尤溪，作诗。作品：《自沙县抵龙（一作尤）溪县值泉州军过后村落皆空因有一绝（此后庚午年）》<div id='poem_49015' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_49015' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/49015?labeling=true' target='_blank'>自沙县抵龙<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作尤）</span>溪县值泉州军过后村落皆空因有一绝<span class='inlineComment2'>（此后庚午年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（910年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐末 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21436, "唐末", "韩偓", "poem_title_49015")'>韩偓</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_49015_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_49015'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_49015'>水自潺湲日自斜，尽无鸡犬有<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_49015", 49015, "Clauses/1/Comments/0")'>鸣鸦</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_0_49015_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_49015'>千村万落如寒食，不见人烟空见花。<div id='poem_sentence_1_49015_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_49015'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_49015_comment'></div></div><div class='poemComment' id='poem_comment_49015'><a href='javascript: ShowPoemComment(49015)'>评注</a><span class='inlineComment4'>（点击查看或隐藏评注）</span></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>韩偓有感而发，作诗。作品：《多情》<div id='poem_49139' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_49139' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/49139?labeling=true' target='_blank'>多情<span class='inlineComment2'>（庚午年在桃林场作）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（910年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐末 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21436, "唐末", "韩偓", "poem_title_49139")'>韩偓</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_49139_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_49139'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_49139'>天遣多情不自持，多情兼与病相宜。<div id='poem_sentence_0_49139_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_49139'>蜂偷野<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作崖）</span>蜜初尝处，莺啄含桃欲咽时。<div id='poem_sentence_1_49139_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_49139'>酒荡襟怀微<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_49139", 49139, "Clauses/4/Comments/1")'>駊騀</span><span class='inlineComment2'>（一作叵我）</span>，春牵情绪更<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作正）</span>融怡。<div id='poem_sentence_2_49139_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_49139'>水香剩置<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作贮，一作注）</span>金盆<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作杯）</span>里，琼树长须<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作须长）</span>浸一枝。<div id='poem_sentence_3_49139_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_49139'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_49139_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; -----title
南安
-----detail

id='poem_sentence_3_49268'>虚空无障处，蒙闭有开时。<div id='poem_sentence_3_49268_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_49268'>苇鹭怜潇洒，泥䲡畏日<span id='poem_sentence_0_49232_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_49232'>清宵玩月唯红叶，永日关门但绿苔。<div id='poem_sentence_1_49232_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' class='inlineComment2'>（一作毵）</span>白</span>离情高处切，腻香<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作红）</span>愁态静中深。<div id='poem_sentence_0_49224_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_49224'>眼随片片沿流去，恨满枝枝被雨淋<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作侵）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_49224_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_49224'>总得苔遮犹慰意，若教泥污更伤心。<div id='poem_sentence_2_49224_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_49224'>临轩<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作阶）</span>一盏悲春酒，明日池塘是绿阴。<div id='poem_sentence_3_49224_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_49224'></div><div class='inlineComment2'>（一作漾）</span>花归别涧<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作浦）</span>，断云含雨入孤村。<div id='poem_sentence_1_49191_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_49191'>人闲易有<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作得）</span>芳时恨，地胜<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作迥）</span>难招自古魂。<div id='poem_sentence_2_49191_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_49191'>惭愧流莺相厚意，清晨犹为到西园。<div id='poem_sentence_3_49191_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_49191'></div><div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=917&endYear=922')">917-922年</a>　在南安，姑系于此。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=923&endYear=923')">923年</a>　韩偓卒于南安葵山之鹿的龙兴寺院。同年，后梁灭于后唐。<br
